/**
 * 知己 · 管理后台 - 测试记录页
 */

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from "react"
import { ClipboardList, Trash2, ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, Filter } from "lucide-react"

interface TestRecord {
  _id: string
  userId: string
  testType: string
  resultType: string
  resultTypeName: string
  scores: Record<string, number>
  createdAt: string
}

export default function AdminTestRecordsPage() {
  const [records, setRecords] = useState<TestRecord[]>([])
  const [total, setTotal] = useState(0)
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1)
  const [testType, setTestType] = useState("")
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const pageSize = 20

  const fetchRecords = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    try {
      const params = new URLSearchParams({ page: String(page), pageSize: String(pageSize) })
      if (testType) params.set("type", testType)
      const res = await fetch(`/api/admin/test-records?${params}`)
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) {
        setRecords(data.data.list)
        setTotal(data.data.total)
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("获取测试记录失败:", err)
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }, [page, testType])

  useEffect(() => { fetchRecords() }, [fetchRecords])

  const handleDelete = async (id: string) => {
    if (!confirm("确定要删除该记录吗？")) return
    try {
      await fetch(`/api/admin/test-records?id=${id}`, { method: "DELETE" })
      fetchRecords()
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("删除失败:", err)
    }
  }

  const typeLabels: Record<string, string> = { mbti: "MBTI", enneagram: "九型人格", numerology: "数字生命密码" }
  const typeColors: Record<string, string> = { mbti: "text-violet-400 bg-violet-500/10", enneagram: "text-emerald-400 bg-emerald-500/10", numerology: "text-amber-400 bg-amber-500/10" }
  const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / pageSize)

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">测试记录</h1>
        <div className="text-sm text-slate-400">共 {total} 条记录</div>
      </div>

      {/* 筛选 */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <Filter className="w-4 h-4 text-slate-500" />
        {["", "mbti", "enneagram", "numerology"].map((t) => (
          <button
            key={t}
            onClick={() => { setTestType(t); setPage(1) }}
            className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors ${testType === t ? "bg-cyan-500/20 text-cyan-400 border border-cyan-500/30" : "bg-slate-800/50 text-slate-400 border border-slate-700/50 hover:border-slate-600/50"}`}
          >
            {t ? typeLabels[t] : "全部"}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* 记录表格 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
        <table className="w-full">
          <thead>
            <tr className="border-b border-slate-700/50">
              <th className="text-left text-xs text-slate-400 font-medium px-4 py-3">测试类型</th>
              <th className="text-left text-xs text-slate-400 font-medium px-4 py-3">结果</th>
              <th className="text-left text-xs text-slate-400 font-medium px-4 py-3">用户ID</th>
              <th className="text-left text-xs text-slate-400 font-medium px-4 py-3">测试时间</th>
              <th className="text-left text-xs text-slate-400 font-medium px-4 py-3">操作</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            {loading ? (
              Array.from({ length: 5 }).map((_, i) => (
                <tr key={i} className="border-b border-slate-700/30">
                  <td colSpan={5} className="px-4 py-4"><div className="h-4 bg-slate-700/50 rounded animate-pulse" /></td>
                </tr>
              ))
            ) : records.length > 0 ? (
              records.map((record) => (
                <tr key={record._id} className="border-b border-slate-700/30 hover:bg-slate-700/20">
                  <td className="px-4 py-3">
                    <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs ${typeColors[record.testType] || "text-slate-400 bg-slate-600/50"}`}>
                      {typeLabels[record.testType] || record.testType}
                    </span>
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-200">{record.resultTypeName || record.resultType || "-"}</td>
                  <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-400 font-mono">{(record.userId || "").slice(0, 12)}...</td>
                  <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-500">{(record.createdAt || "").replace("T", " ").slice(0, 19)}</td>
                  <td className="px-4 py-3">
                    <button onClick={() => handleDelete(record._id)} className="p-1.5 rounded hover:bg-red-500/10 text-slate-400 hover:text-red-400">
                      <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
                    </button>
                  </td>
                </tr>
              ))
            ) : (
              <tr>
                <td colSpan={5} className="px-4 py-12 text-center text-slate-500 text-sm">暂无测试记录</td>
              </tr>
            )}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>

      {/* 分页 */}
      {totalPages > 1 && (
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-500">第 {page} / {totalPages} 页</span>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <button onClick={() => setPage(Math.max(1, page - 1))} disabled={page <= 1} className="p-2 rounded-lg bg-slate-800/50 text-slate-400 hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-30">
              <ChevronLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
            </button>
            <button onClick={() => setPage(Math.min(totalPages, page + 1))} disabled={page >= totalPages} className="p-2 rounded-lg bg-slate-800/50 text-slate-400 hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-30">
              <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

/**
 * 知己 · 管理后台 - AI设置页
 * 配置AI服务商、模型、提示词模板、老师匹配规则
 */

import { useState, useEffect } from "react"
import { Brain, Save, RefreshCw, Eye, EyeOff } from "lucide-react"

interface AISettings {
  provider: string
  apiKey: string
  baseUrl: string
  model: string
  maxTokens: number
  temperature: number
  prompts: Record<string, string>
  matchSettings: { enabled: boolean; matchPrompt: string }
}

export default function AdminAISettingsPage() {
  const [settings, setSettings] = useState<AISettings | null>(null)
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
  const [showApiKey, setShowApiKey] = useState(false)
  const [activePromptTab, setActivePromptTab] = useState("mbti")
  const [saved, setSaved] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => { fetchSettings() }, [])

  const fetchSettings = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/admin/ai-settings")
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) setSettings(data.data)
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("获取AI设置失败:", err)
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }

  const handleSave = async () => {
    if (!settings) return
    setSaving(true)
    try {
      await fetch("/api/admin/ai-settings", {
        method: "PUT",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(settings),
      })
      setSaved(true)
      setTimeout(() => setSaved(false), 2000)
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("保存失败:", err)
    } finally {
      setSaving(false)
    }
  }

  const promptTabs = [
    { key: "mbti", label: "MBTI" },
    { key: "enneagram", label: "九型人格" },
    { key: "numerology", label: "数字生命密码" },
  ]

  if (loading || !settings) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">AI设置</h1>
        <div className="bg-slate-800/50 rounded-xl p-6 animate-pulse">
          <div className="h-6 bg-slate-700 rounded w-32 mb-4" />
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {[1, 2, 3, 4].map((i) => <div key={i} className="h-10 bg-slate-700 rounded" />)}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">AI设置</h1>
        <button
          onClick={handleSave}
          disabled={saving}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 bg-cyan-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-cyan-400 transition-colors text-sm disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          {saving ? <RefreshCw className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Save className="w-4 h-4" />}
          {saved ? "已保存 ✓" : "保存设置"}
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* AI服务配置 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-6">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-6">
          <Brain className="w-5 h-5 text-cyan-400" />
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">AI服务配置</h2>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-slate-400 mb-1">服务商</label>
            <select
              value={settings.provider}
              onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, provider: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-3 py-2.5 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50"
            >
              <option value="groq">Groq</option>
              <option value="openai">OpenAI</option>
              <option value="coze">Coze（扣子）</option>
              <option value="zhipu">智谱AI</option>
            </select>
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-slate-400 mb-1">模型</label>
            <input
              value={settings.model}
              onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, model: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-3 py-2.5 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50"
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-slate-400 mb-1">API Key</label>
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type={showApiKey ? "text" : "password"}
                value={settings.apiKey}
                onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, apiKey: e.target.value })}
                placeholder="sk-..."
                className="w-full px-3 py-2.5 pr-10 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50"
              />
              <button onClick={() => setShowApiKey(!showApiKey)} className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-500">
                {showApiKey ? <EyeOff className="w-4 h-4" /> : <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-slate-400 mb-1">API Base URL</label>
            <input
              value={settings.baseUrl}
              onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, baseUrl: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-3 py-2.5 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50"
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-slate-400 mb-1">最大Token数</label>
            <input
              type="number"
              value={settings.maxTokens}
              onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, maxTokens: parseInt(e.target.value) || 4096 })}
              className="w-full px-3 py-2.5 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50"
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-slate-400 mb-1">温度（0-1）</label>
            <input
              type="number"
              step="0.1"
              min="0"
              max="1"
              value={settings.temperature}
              onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, temperature: parseFloat(e.target.value) || 0.7 })}
              className="w-full px-3 py-2.5 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50"
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* AI提示词模板 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-6">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white mb-4">解读提示词模板</h2>

        {/* Tab 切换 */}
        <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
          {promptTabs.map((tab) => (
            <button
              key={tab.key}
              onClick={() => setActivePromptTab(tab.key)}
              className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors ${activePromptTab === tab.key ? "bg-cyan-500/20 text-cyan-400 border border-cyan-500/30" : "bg-slate-700/50 text-slate-400 border border-slate-600/50"}`}
            >
              {tab.label}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        <textarea
          value={settings.prompts[activePromptTab] || ""}
          onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, prompts: { ...settings.prompts, [activePromptTab]: e.target.value } })}
          rows={6}
          className="w-full px-4 py-3 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm leading-relaxed focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50 resize-none"
          placeholder="输入AI解读提示词模板..."
        />
      </div>

      {/* AI匹配老师设置 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-6">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">AI匹配老师设置</h2>
          <button
            onClick={() => setSettings({
              ...settings,
              matchSettings: { ...settings.matchSettings, enabled: !settings.matchSettings.enabled },
            })}
            className={`relative w-12 h-6 rounded-full transition-colors ${settings.matchSettings.enabled ? "bg-cyan-500" : "bg-slate-600"}`}
          >
            <span className={`absolute top-0.5 w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-white transition-transform ${settings.matchSettings.enabled ? "left-6" : "left-0.5"}`} />
          </button>
        </div>

        {settings.matchSettings.enabled && (
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-slate-400 mb-2">匹配提示词</label>
            <textarea
              value={settings.matchSettings.matchPrompt}
              onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, matchSettings: { ...settings.matchSettings, matchPrompt: e.target.value } })}
              rows={3}
              className="w-full px-4 py-3 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50 resize-none"
            />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/admin/settings/page.tsx

/**
 * 知己 · 管理后台 - 系统设置页
 * 全局配置：站点信息、测评设置、咨询设置、推荐绑定、积分设置
 */

import { useState, useEffect } from "react"
import { Settings, Save, RefreshCw } from "lucide-react"

interface SystemSettings {
  siteName: string
  siteDescription: string
  logo: string
  freeTestCount: number
  testCooldown: number
  consultPrice: number
  consultDuration: number
  referralBindingDays: number
  referralCommission: number
  referralEnabled: boolean
  registerPoints: number
  testPoints: number
  invitePoints: number
}

export default function AdminSettingsPage() {
  const [settings, setSettings] = useState<SystemSettings | null>(null)
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
  const [saved, setSaved] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => { fetchSettings() }, [])

  const fetchSettings = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/admin/settings")
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) setSettings(data.data)
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("获取设置失败:", err)
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }

  const handleSave = async () => {
    if (!settings) return
    setSaving(true)
    try {
      await fetch("/api/admin/settings", {
        method: "PUT",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(settings),
      })
      setSaved(true)
      setTimeout(() => setSaved(false), 2000)
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("保存失败:", err)
    } finally {
      setSaving(false)
    }
  }

  if (loading || !settings) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">系统设置</h1>
        <div className="bg-slate-800/50 rounded-xl p-6 animate-pulse space-y-3">
          {[1, 2, 3, 4].map((i) => <div key={i} className="h-10 bg-slate-700 rounded" />)}
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  /** 设置项组件 */
  const SettingRow = ({ label, desc, children }: { label: string; desc?: string; children: React.ReactNode }) => (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between py-4 border-b border-slate-700/30 last:border-0">
      <div className="flex-1 mr-6">
        <div className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-200">{label}</div>
        {desc && <div className="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-0.5">{desc}</div>}
      </div>
      <div className="flex-shrink-0">{children}</div>
    </div>
  )

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">系统设置</h1>
        <button
          onClick={handleSave}
          disabled={saving}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 bg-cyan-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-cyan-400 transition-colors text-sm disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          {saving ? <RefreshCw className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Save className="w-4 h-4" />}
          {saved ? "已保存 ✓" : "保存设置"}
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* 站点信息 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-6">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white mb-4 flex items-center gap-2">
          <Settings className="w-5 h-5 text-cyan-400" />
          站点信息
        </h2>
        <SettingRow label="站点名称">
          <input value={settings.siteName} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, siteName: e.target.value })} className="w-48 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
        <SettingRow label="站点描述">
          <input value={settings.siteDescription} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, siteDescription: e.target.value })} className="w-64 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
      </div>

      {/* 测评设置 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-6">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white mb-4">测评设置</h2>
        <SettingRow label="每种测评免费次数" desc="用户首次测评免费次数">
          <input type="number" value={settings.freeTestCount} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, freeTestCount: parseInt(e.target.value) || 1 })} className="w-24 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
        <SettingRow label="重复测试冷却时间" desc="同一测评再次测试的等待时间（小时）">
          <input type="number" value={settings.testCooldown} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, testCooldown: parseInt(e.target.value) || 24 })} className="w-24 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
      </div>

      {/* 咨询设置 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-6">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white mb-4">咨询设置</h2>
        <SettingRow label="默认咨询价格（元/次）">
          <input type="number" value={settings.consultPrice} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, consultPrice: parseInt(e.target.value) || 398 })} className="w-24 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
        <SettingRow label="默认咨询时长（分钟）">
          <input type="number" value={settings.consultDuration} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, consultDuration: parseInt(e.target.value) || 60 })} className="w-24 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
      </div>

      {/* 推荐绑定设置 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-6">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">推荐绑定设置</h2>
          <button
            onClick={() => setSettings({ ...settings, referralEnabled: !settings.referralEnabled })}
            className={`relative w-12 h-6 rounded-full transition-colors ${settings.referralEnabled ? "bg-cyan-500" : "bg-slate-600"}`}
          >
            <span className={`absolute top-0.5 w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-white transition-transform ${settings.referralEnabled ? "left-6" : "left-0.5"}`} />
          </button>
        </div>
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 mb-4">参考 Soul 项目 30 天绑定规则：谁发的链接进的人就绑谁，一级分销，绑定有效期 30 天</p>
        <SettingRow label="绑定有效期（天）" desc="推荐绑定关系的有效天数">
          <input type="number" value={settings.referralBindingDays} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, referralBindingDays: parseInt(e.target.value) || 30 })} className="w-24 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
        <SettingRow label="推荐佣金比例" desc="推荐人获得的佣金百分比">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <input type="number" step="0.01" value={settings.referralCommission} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, referralCommission: parseFloat(e.target.value) || 0.1 })} className="w-20 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
            <span className="text-sm text-slate-400">({Math.round(settings.referralCommission * 100)}%)</span>
          </div>
        </SettingRow>
      </div>

      {/* 积分设置 */}
      <div className="bg-slate-800/50 backdrop-blur rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-6">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white mb-4">积分设置</h2>
        <SettingRow label="注册赠送积分">
          <input type="number" value={settings.registerPoints} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, registerPoints: parseInt(e.target.value) || 0 })} className="w-24 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
        <SettingRow label="完成测评赠送积分">
          <input type="number" value={settings.testPoints} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, testPoints: parseInt(e.target.value) || 0 })} className="w-24 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
        <SettingRow label="邀请好友赠送积分">
          <input type="number" value={settings.invitePoints} onChange={(e) => setSettings({ ...settings, invitePoints: parseInt(e.target.value) || 0 })} className="w-24 px-3 py-2 bg-slate-700/50 border border-slate-600/50 rounded-lg text-white text-sm text-center focus:outline-none focus:border-cyan-500/50" />
        </SettingRow>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

assistant:
现在创建推荐绑定 API（参考 Soul 项目的30天绑定机制）。
[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/api/referral/bind/route.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 推荐绑定 API
 * 参考 Soul 项目的 30天绑定规则：
 * 1. 链接带ID：谁发的链接，进的人就绑谁
 * 2. 一级、一月：只有一级分销，绑定有效期30天
 * 3. 长期不发：别人发得多，客户会被「抢走」
 * 4. 每天发：持续发的人绑定一直有效
 * 5. 约10%给分发：推荐佣金比例
 *
 * POST: 创建/续期/抢夺绑定
 * GET: 查询绑定状态
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"

/** POST - 创建推荐绑定 */
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json()
    const { referrerId, refereeId, referralCode, source } = body

    if (!referrerId || !refereeId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "缺少必要参数" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    // 不能自己推荐自己
    if (referrerId === refereeId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "不能推荐自己" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const collection = db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REFERRAL_BINDINGS)
    const now = new Date()

    // 获取系统设置中的绑定天数
    const settingsDoc = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.SYSTEM_SETTINGS).findOne({ key: "system_config" })
    const bindingDays = settingsDoc?.config?.referralBindingDays || 30
    const expiryDate = new Date(now.getTime() + bindingDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)

    // 查找现有绑定
    const existingBinding = await collection.findOne({
      refereeId,
      status: "active",
    })

    let action: "new" | "renew" | "takeover" = "new"

    if (existingBinding) {
      const existingExpiry = new Date(existingBinding.expiryDate)

      if (existingBinding.referrerId === referrerId) {
        // 同一推荐人 → 续期
        action = "renew"
        await collection.updateOne(
          { _id: existingBinding._id },
          {
            $set: {
              expiryDate: expiryDate.toISOString(),
              lastRenewDate: now.toISOString(),
              renewCount: (existingBinding.renewCount || 0) + 1,
              updatedAt: now.toISOString(),
            },
          }
        )
      } else if (existingExpiry < now) {
        // 已过期 → 可以被抢夺
        action = "takeover"
        // 将旧绑定标记为过期
        await collection.updateOne(
          { _id: existingBinding._id },
          { $set: { status: "expired", updatedAt: now.toISOString() } }
        )
      } else {
        // 未过期且不是同一推荐人 → 不能绑定
        return NextResponse.json({
          success: false,
          error: "用户已绑定其他推荐人，绑定有效期内无法更换",
          data: {
            currentReferrerId: existingBinding.referrerId,
            expiryDate: existingBinding.expiryDate,
          },
        })
      }
    }

    // 创建新绑定（new 或 takeover）
    if (action === "new" || action === "takeover") {
      await collection.insertOne({
        referrerId,
        refereeId,
        referralCode: referralCode || "",
        source: source || "link", // link/poster/qrcode/miniprogram
        status: "active",
        action,
        bindingDate: now.toISOString(),
        expiryDate: expiryDate.toISOString(),
        renewCount: 0,
        conversionDate: null,
        commissionAmount: 0,
        orderId: null,
        createdAt: now.toISOString(),
        updatedAt: now.toISOString(),
      })
    }

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        action,
        referrerId,
        refereeId,
        expiryDate: expiryDate.toISOString(),
        bindingDays,
      },
    })
  } catch (error: unknown) {
    console.error("[知己] 推荐绑定失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "绑定失败" }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/** GET - 查询绑定状态 */
export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
    const refereeId = searchParams.get("refereeId")
    const referrerId = searchParams.get("referrerId")

    if (!refereeId && !referrerId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "请提供 refereeId 或 referrerId" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const collection = db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REFERRAL_BINDINGS)

    const query: Record<string, unknown> = {}
    if (refereeId) query.refereeId = refereeId
    if (referrerId) query.referrerId = referrerId

    const bindings = await collection.find(query).sort({ createdAt: -1 }).limit(50).toArray()

    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, data: { list: bindings } })
  } catch (error: unknown) {
    console.error("[知己] 查询绑定失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, data: { list: [] } })
  }
}

          data: { token, admin: { id: "default_admin", username: "admin", role: "superadmin", nickname: "超级管理员" } },
        })
      }
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "用户名或密码错误" }, { status: 401 })
    }

    // 查找管理员
    const collection = db.collection(COLLECTIONS.ADMIN_USERS)

    // 首次启动：初始化默认管理员
    const count = await collection.countDocuments()
    if (count === 0) {
      await collection.insertOne({
        username: "admin",
        password: hashPassword("admin123"),
        nickname: "超级管理员",
        role: "superadmin",
        status: "active",
        createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      console.log("[知己Admin] 已创建默认管理员: admin/admin123")
    }

    // 验证登录
    const admin = await collection.findOne({ username, status: "active" })
    if (!admin) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "用户名或密码错误" }, { status: 401 })
    }

    const hashedPwd = hashPassword(password)
    if (admin.password !== hashedPwd) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "用户名或密码错误" }, { status: 401 })
    }

    // 生成 token
    const token = generateToken(String(admin._id), admin.username)

    // 更新最后登录时间
    await collection.updateOne({ _id: admin._id }, { $set: { lastLoginAt: new Date().toISOString() } })

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        token,
        admin: {
          id: String(admin._id),
          username: admin.username,
          nickname: admin.nickname,
          role: admin.role,
        },
      },
    })
  new_string:     // 先尝试 MongoDB 认证
    let usedDb = false
    try {
      const conn = await connectToDatabase()
      const db = conn.db
      const collection = db.collection(COLLECTIONS.ADMIN_USERS)

      // 首次启动：初始化默认管理员
      const count = await collection.countDocuments()
      if (count === 0) {
        await collection.insertOne({
          username: "admin",
          password: hashPassword("admin123"),
          nickname: "超级管理员",
          role: "superadmin",
          status: "active",
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        })
        console.log("[知己Admin] 已创建默认管理员: admin/admin123")
      }

      // 验证登录
      const admin = await collection.findOne({ username, status: "active" })
      if (admin) {
        const hashedPwd = hashPassword(password)
        if (admin.password === hashedPwd) {
          usedDb = true
          const token = generateToken(String(admin._id), admin.username)
          await collection.updateOne({ _id: admin._id }, { $set: { lastLoginAt: new Date().toISOString() } })
          return NextResponse.json({
            success: true,
            data: {
              token,
              admin: { id: String(admin._id), username: admin.username, nickname: admin.nickname, role: admin.role },
            },
          })
        }
      }

      // 数据库中没找到匹配的管理员
      if (count > 0) {
        return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "用户名或密码错误" }, { status: 401 })
      }
    } catch (dbError) {
      console.log("[知己Admin] MongoDB不可用，使用本地认证:", (dbError as Error).message?.slice(0, 50))
    }

    // MongoDB不可用或无数据时，使用内置默认管理员账号
    if (!usedDb && username === "admin" && password === "admin123") {
      const token = generateToken("default_admin", "admin")
      return NextResponse.json({
        success: true,
        data: { token, admin: { id: "default_admin", username: "admin", role: "superadmin", nickname: "超级管理员" } },
      })
    }

    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "用户名或密码错误" }, { status: 401 })

## 变更日志

### 2026-02-10（管理后台 + 测评重构）
- **重构** 测评体系：从4种(MBTI/PDP/DISC/盖洛普)调整为3种(MBTI/九型人格/数字生命密码)

- **新增** 数字生命密码：基于生日计算生命灵数(1-9+11/22/33)，含五行/情感/职业解读
- **更新** 首页：性格测评入口改为3项竖向列表，移除"数字能量"待上线模块
- **更新** 测评中心：支持生日输入模式（数字生命密码）
- **新增** 管理后台完整系统（/admin）：
  - 登录认证（默认 admin / admin123，支持MongoDB降级）
  - 数据概览仪表盘（实时统计+最近用户+最近测试）
  - 用户管理（CRUD + 搜索 + 分页）
  - 题库管理（3套测评展示 + 编辑 + 导入）
  - 咨询师管理（入驻 + 编辑 + 测评匹配关联 + 上下线状态）
  - 测试记录管理（列表 + 类型筛选 + 删除）
  - AI设置（服务商/模型/API Key/提示词模板/匹配规则）
  - 系统设置（测评/咨询/推荐绑定/积分全局配置）
- **新增** 管理后台API（7个端点）：
  - /api/admin/auth - 管理员认证
  - /api/admin/dashboard - 仪表盘统计
  - /api/admin/users - 用户CRUD
  - /api/admin/questions - 题库CRUD
  - /api/admin/consultants - 咨询师CRUD
  - /api/admin/ai-settings - AI配置
  - /api/admin/settings - 系统设置
  - /api/admin/test-records - 测试记录管理
- **新增** 推荐绑定API（/api/referral/bind）：参考Soul项目30天绑定规则
- **新增** MongoDB集合：admin_users/question_banks/ai_settings/system_settings/referral_bindings

## 经验速查表
  new_string: ### 7. 管理后台完整开发流程
**问题**：需要从零构建知己管理后台（参考Soul和MBTI项目）
**解决方案**：
- 参考 Soul 项目的深色主题 + 侧边栏布局
- 参考 MBTI 项目的题库管理 + 用户管理模式
- API全部实现优雅降级（MongoDB不可用时返回空数据或默认配置）
- 默认管理员 admin/admin123 在首次访问时自动创建
**关键步骤**：
1. 先建 API Routes（auth → dashboard → users → questions → consultants → ai-settings → settings）
2. 再建前端页面（layout → login → page → 各子页面）
3. 所有CRUD操作统一使用 MongoDB ObjectId
4. 前后端数据字段保持一致

### 8. 测评体系重构（4种→3种）
**问题**：从MBTI/PDP/DISC/盖洛普调整为MBTI/九型人格/数字生命密码
**解决方案**：
- MBTI保持不变（28题）
- 九型人格：36题（4题×9型），计算得分最高的类型为主型
- 数字生命密码：inputType="birthday"，通过生日计算生命灵数（1-9/11/22/33）
- test-page.tsx 新增生日输入模式渲染分支
**关键点**：TestConfig 新增 `inputType?: "questions" | "birthday"` 字段区分

### 9. 推荐绑定30天机制（参考Soul项目）
**问题**：需要实现用户推荐绑定和锁定机制
**解决方案**：参考Soul项目的核心规则
- 谁发的链接，进的人就绑谁
- 一级分销，绑定有效期30天
- 同一推荐人可续期，不同推荐人在过期后可抢夺
- 未过期且不同推荐人则无法绑定
**关键代码**：`/api/referral/bind/route.ts`
**绑定状态**：new（新绑定）、renew（续期）、takeover（抢夺）

### 10. MongoDB 认证问题处理
**问题**：本地MongoDB启用了认证，直接连接报 Unauthorized
**解决方案**：
- auth API 的 catch 块处理 MongoDB 认证失败
- 降级到内置默认管理员账号（admin/admin123）
- 所有管理后台 API 都有 try-catch 降级
**教训**：不能假设 MongoDB 一定无认证，所有数据库操作必须有降级方案

---

【知己 · 复盘】

**目标&结果**：开发知己项目的完整管理后台 + 重构测评体系 → 全部完成

**过程**：
1. **测评重构**：从4种测评(MBTI/PDP/DISC/盖洛普)调整为3种(MBTI/九型人格/数字生命密码)，搜索GitHub九型人格题库参考，创建36题完整题库，数字生命密码实现生日计算逻辑
2. **管理后台API**：8个API端点全部开发完成（认证/仪表盘/用户/题库/咨询师/测试记录/AI设置/系统设置），所有API实现MongoDB优雅降级
3. **管理后台页面**：7个功能页面（深色主题+侧边栏，参考Soul和MBTI项目），包含登录、仪表盘、用户/题库/咨询师CRUD、AI设置、系统设置
4. **推荐绑定**：参考Soul项目30天绑定规则实现了 new/renew/takeover 三种绑定状态
5. **前端更新**：首页改为3个测评竖向卡片，测评中心新增生日输入模式
6. **验证测试**：admin/admin123 登录API验证通过（curl），管理后台各页面正常加载

**反思**：
- 本地MongoDB需要认证，导致初次登录500错误 → 已修复auth API的降级逻辑
- 浏览器自动化测试中表单提交存在React受控输入兼容问题 → API通过curl验证通过

**总结**：管理后台7大功能模块全部就绪，前后端数据字段一致，默认admin/admin123可直接登录

**下一步**：
- 修复管理后台登录页的浏览器表单提交问题
- 接入真实LLM（配置AI_API_KEY）
- JWT认证中间件
- 微信支付对接

/**
 * 知己 · 管理后台布局
 * 亮色暖色调（米黄色/珊瑚色）与首页风格一致
 * 侧边栏导航 + 顶部标题栏
 */

import { useState, useEffect } from "react"
import { usePathname, useRouter } from "next/navigation"
import {
  LayoutDashboard, Users, BookOpen, UserCheck, Brain, Settings,
  LogOut, Menu, X, ClipboardList, ChevronRight, CreditCard, Sparkles,
} from "lucide-react"

/** 侧边栏菜单项 */
const menuItems = [
  { key: "dashboard", label: "数据概览", icon: LayoutDashboard, href: "/admin" },
  { key: "users", label: "用户管理", icon: Users, href: "/admin/users" },
  { key: "questions", label: "题库管理", icon: BookOpen, href: "/admin/questions" },
  { key: "consultants", label: "咨询师管理", icon: UserCheck, href: "/admin/consultants" },
  { key: "test-records", label: "测试记录", icon: ClipboardList, href: "/admin/test-records" },
  { key: "ai-settings", label: "AI设置", icon: Brain, href: "/admin/ai-settings" },
  { key: "payment", label: "支付配置", icon: CreditCard, href: "/admin/payment" },
  { key: "settings", label: "系统设置", icon: Settings, href: "/admin/settings" },
]

export default function AdminLayout({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(true)
  const [isLoggedIn, setIsLoggedIn] = useState(false)
  const [adminInfo, setAdminInfo] = useState<{ username: string; nickname: string } | null>(null)
  const pathname = usePathname()
  const router = useRouter()

  // 检查登录状态
  useEffect(() => {
    const token = localStorage.getItem("zhiji_admin_token")
    const admin = localStorage.getItem("zhiji_admin_info")
    if (token && admin) {
      setIsLoggedIn(true)
      try { setAdminInfo(JSON.parse(admin)) } catch { /* 忽略 */ }
    } else if (pathname !== "/admin/login") {
      router.push("/admin/login")
    }
  }, [pathname, router])

  // 登录页不使用后台布局
  if (pathname === "/admin/login") {
    return <>{children}</>
  }

  // 未登录时显示加载
  if (!isLoggedIn) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50 flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="animate-spin w-8 h-8 border-2 border-coral border-t-transparent rounded-full" />
      </div>
    )
  }

  const handleLogout = () => {
    localStorage.removeItem("zhiji_admin_token")
    localStorage.removeItem("zhiji_admin_info")
    router.push("/admin/login")
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50 text-foreground flex">
      {/* 侧边栏 - 暖色毛玻璃风格 */}
      <aside
        className={`fixed lg:static inset-y-0 left-0 z-50 flex flex-col transition-all duration-300 bg-white/80 backdrop-blur-xl border-r border-orange-100 shadow-lg shadow-orange-100/20 ${
          sidebarOpen ? "w-64" : "w-16"
        }`}
      >
        {/* Logo */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between h-16 px-4 border-b border-orange-100">
          {sidebarOpen && (
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-coral to-orange flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold text-sm shadow-md shadow-coral/20">
                知
              </div>
              <span className="font-bold text-lg bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-orange bg-clip-text text-transparent">
                知己管理后台
              </span>
            </div>
          )}
          <button
            onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(!sidebarOpen)}
            className="p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-orange-50 text-muted-foreground"
          >
            {sidebarOpen ? <X className="w-5 h-5" /> : <Menu className="w-5 h-5" />}
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* 菜单列表 */}
        <nav className="flex-1 py-4 space-y-1 px-2 overflow-y-auto">
          {menuItems.map((item) => {
            const Icon = item.icon
            const isActive = pathname === item.href || (item.href !== "/admin" && pathname.startsWith(item.href))
            return (
              <button
                key={item.key}
                onClick={() => router.push(item.href)}
                className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-xl transition-all duration-200 group ${
                  isActive
                    ? "bg-gradient-to-r from-coral/10 to-orange/10 text-coral border border-coral/20 shadow-sm"
                    : "text-muted-foreground hover:bg-orange-50 hover:text-foreground"
                }`}
              >
                <Icon className={`w-5 h-5 flex-shrink-0 ${isActive ? "text-coral" : ""}`} />
                {sidebarOpen && (
                  <>
                    <span className="text-sm font-medium">{item.label}</span>
                    {isActive && <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4 ml-auto text-coral" />}
                  </>
                )}
              </button>
            )
          })}
        </nav>

        {/* 底部用户信息 */}
        <div className="border-t border-orange-100 p-4">
          {sidebarOpen ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-coral to-gold flex items-center justify-center text-xs text-white font-medium shadow-md">
                  {adminInfo?.nickname?.charAt(0) || "A"}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm">
                  <div className="font-medium text-foreground">{adminInfo?.nickname || "管理员"}</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{adminInfo?.username || "admin"}</div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <button onClick={handleLogout} className="p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-red-50 text-muted-foreground hover:text-red-500" title="退出登录">
                <LogOut className="w-4 h-4" />
              </button>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <button onClick={handleLogout} className="w-full flex justify-center p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-red-50 text-muted-foreground hover:text-red-500">
              <LogOut className="w-5 h-5" />
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </aside>

      {/* 主内容区 */}
      <main className="flex-1 min-h-screen overflow-auto">
        {/* 顶部栏 */}
        <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 h-16 border-b border-orange-100 bg-white/80 backdrop-blur-xl flex items-center justify-between px-6">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            <Sparkles className="w-4 h-4 text-coral" />
            <span>知己管理后台</span>
            <ChevronRight className="w-3 h-3" />
            <span className="text-foreground font-medium">
              {menuItems.find((m) => m.href === pathname || (m.href !== "/admin" && pathname.startsWith(m.href)))?.label || "数据概览"}
            </span>
          </div>
          <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            {new Date().toLocaleDateString("zh-CN", { year: "numeric", month: "long", day: "numeric", weekday: "long" })}
          </div>
        </header>

        {/* 页面内容 */}
        <div className="p-6">{children}</div>
      </main>
    </div>
  )
}

/**
 * 知己 · 管理后台登录页
 * 暖色调风格（与首页一致）
 * 默认账号：admin / admin123
 */

import { useState } from "react"
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation"
import { Eye, EyeOff, Lock, User, Sparkles } from "lucide-react"

export default function AdminLoginPage() {
  const [username, setUsername] = useState("")
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("")
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false)
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState("")
  const router = useRouter()

  const handleLogin = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    if (!username || !password) { setError("请输入用户名和密码"); return }
    setLoading(true); setError("")
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/admin/auth", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ username, password }),
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) {
        localStorage.setItem("zhiji_admin_token", data.data.token)
        localStorage.setItem("zhiji_admin_info", JSON.stringify(data.data.admin))
        router.push("/admin")
      } else {
        setError(data.error || "登录失败")
      }
    } catch { setError("网络错误，请稍后重试") }
    finally { setLoading(false) }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4">
      {/* 背景装饰 */}
      <div className="fixed inset-0 pointer-events-none overflow-hidden">
        <div className="absolute -top-40 -right-40 w-96 h-96 bg-gradient-to-br from-coral/10 to-orange/10 rounded-full blur-3xl" />
        <div className="absolute top-1/3 -left-20 w-72 h-72 bg-gradient-to-br from-gold/10 to-amber-500/5 rounded-full blur-3xl" />
        <div className="absolute bottom-20 right-20 w-48 h-48 bg-gradient-to-br from-orange/10 to-coral/10 rounded-full blur-2xl" />
      </div>

      <div className="relative w-full max-w-md">
        {/* Logo */}
        <div className="text-center mb-8">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange to-gold shadow-xl shadow-coral/25 mb-4">
            <Sparkles className="w-8 h-8 text-white" />
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground mb-1">知己 · 管理后台</h1>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">AI驱动的自我探索与咨询平台</p>
        </div>

        {/* 登录表单 */}
        <form
          onSubmit={handleLogin}
          className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur-xl rounded-2xl border border-orange-100 p-8 shadow-xl shadow-orange-100/30"
        >
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground mb-6">管理员登录</h2>

          {error && (
            <div className="mb-4 p-3 bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl text-red-600 text-sm">{error}</div>
          )}

          <div className="mb-4">
            <label className="block text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-2">用户名</label>
            <div className="relative">
              <User className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
              <input
                type="text"
                value={username}
                onChange={(e) => setUsername(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="请输入用户名"
                className="w-full pl-10 pr-4 py-3 bg-orange-50/50 border border-orange-200 rounded-xl text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground/60 focus:outline-none focus:border-coral focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/10 transition-all"
              />
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="mb-6">
            <label className="block text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-2">密码</label>
            <div className="relative">
              <Lock className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
              <input
                type={showPassword ? "text" : "password"}
                value={password}
                onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="请输入密码"
                className="w-full pl-10 pr-12 py-3 bg-orange-50/50 border border-orange-200 rounded-xl text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground/60 focus:outline-none focus:border-coral focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/10 transition-all"
              />
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}
                className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
              >
                {showPassword ? <EyeOff className="w-4 h-4" /> : <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>

          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={loading}
            className="w-full py-3 bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-orange text-white font-medium rounded-xl hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-coral/25 transition-all duration-200 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed"
          >
            {loading ? (
              <span className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
                <span className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-white border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
                登录中...
              </span>
            ) : "登 录"}
          </button>

          <div className="mt-6 text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            默认账号：admin / admin123
          </div>
        </form>

        <div className="mt-8 text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          © 2026 知己 · AI解读与咨询平台 | 存客宝技术支持
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 种子数据API
 * POST: 生成2000个模拟用户数据（含MBTI/九型人格/数字生命密码测试结果）

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"

/** 随机中文名 */
const surnames = ["赵","钱","孙","李","周","吴","郑","王","冯","陈","褚","卫","蒋","沈","韩","杨","朱","秦","尤","许","何","吕","施","张","孔","曹","严","华","金","魏","陶","姜","戚","谢","邹","喻","柏","水","窦","章","云","苏","潘","葛","奚","范","彭","郎","鲁","韦","昌","马","苗","凤","花","方","俞","任","袁","柳","酆","鲍","史","唐","费","廉","岑","薛","雷","贺","倪","汤","滕","殷","罗","毕","郝","邬","安","常","乐","于","时","傅","皮"]
const names = ["伟","芳","娜","敏","静","丽","强","磊","军","洋","勇","艳","杰","娟","涛","明","超","秀英","华","慧","鑫","桂英","玲","婷","建华","建国","子涵","雨晨","浩然","子轩","雨泽","宇轩","梓涵","欣怡","思源","语彤","若曦","佳怡","雅琪","天佑","俊杰","文博","志远","嘉豪","晨曦","子墨","思远","梓萱","紫萱","诗涵"]
const mbtiTypes = ["INTJ","INTP","ENTJ","ENTP","INFJ","INFP","ENFJ","ENFP","ISTJ","ISFJ","ESTJ","ESFJ","ISTP","ISFP","ESTP","ESFP"]
const enneagramTypes = [1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9]
const cities = ["北京","上海","广州","深圳","杭州","成都","重庆","武汉","南京","天津","西安","长沙","厦门","青岛","大连","苏州","郑州","福州","济南","合肥","昆明","贵阳","太原","石家庄","哈尔滨"]

function rand<T>(arr: T[]): T { return arr[Math.floor(Math.random() * arr.length)] }
function randInt(min: number, max: number) { return Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min }
function randPhone() { return `1${rand(["3","5","7","8","9"])}${String(randInt(100000000, 999999999)).padStart(9, "0")}` }
function randDate(start: string, end: string) {
  const s = new Date(start).getTime(), e = new Date(end).getTime()
  return new Date(s + Math.random() * (e - s)).toISOString()
}
function randBirthday() {
  const y = randInt(1970, 2005), m = String(randInt(1, 12)).padStart(2, "0"), d = String(randInt(1, 28)).padStart(2, "0")
  return `${y}-${m}-${d}`
}

/** 计算生命灵数 */
function calcLifePath(birthday: string): number {
  const digits = birthday.replace(/-/g, "")
  const reduce = (n: number): number => {
    while (n > 9 && n !== 11 && n !== 22 && n !== 33) {
      n = String(n).split("").reduce((s, d) => s + parseInt(d), 0)
    }
    return n
  }
  const y = reduce(parseInt(digits.substring(0, 4)))
  const m = reduce(parseInt(digits.substring(4, 6)))
  const d = reduce(parseInt(digits.substring(6, 8)))
  let t = y + m + d
  while (t > 9 && t !== 11 && t !== 22 && t !== 33) {
    t = String(t).split("").reduce((s, c) => s + parseInt(c), 0)
  }
  return t
}

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json()
    const count = Math.min(body.count || 2000, 5000)

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const usersCol = db.collection(COLLECTIONS.USERS)
    const testCol = db.collection(COLLECTIONS.TEST_RECORDS)

    // 生成用户数据
    const users = []
    const testRecords = []

    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      const nickname = rand(surnames) + rand(names)
      const phone = randPhone()
      const birthday = randBirthday()
      const city = rand(cities)
      const mbtiType = rand(mbtiTypes)
      const enneagramType = rand(enneagramTypes)
      const lifePathNumber = calcLifePath(birthday)
      const createdAt = randDate("2025-06-01", "2026-02-10")

      const userId = `user_${Date.now()}_${i}`
      const inviteCode = `ZJ${String(100000 + i).slice(1)}`

      // 用户文档
      users.push({
        id: userId,
        phone,
        nickname,
        avatar: "",
        birthday,
        city,
        gender: rand(["male", "female"]),
        vip: Math.random() < 0.15,
        points: randInt(0, 2000),
        inviteCode,
        referredBy: Math.random() < 0.3 ? `ZJ${String(100000 + randInt(0, Math.max(0, i - 1))).slice(1)}` : "",
        // 测试结果概览
        mbtiType,
        enneagramType: String(enneagramType),
        lifePathNumber: String(lifePathNumber),
        testCount: randInt(1, 6),
        lastTestAt: randDate(createdAt, "2026-02-10"),
        status: Math.random() < 0.95 ? "active" : "inactive",
        createdAt,
        updatedAt: createdAt,
      })

      // MBTI 测试记录
      if (Math.random() < 0.85) {
        const eScore = randInt(1, 7), iScore = 7 - eScore
        const sScore = randInt(1, 7), nScore = 7 - sScore
        const tScore = randInt(1, 7), fScore = 7 - tScore
        const jScore = randInt(1, 7), pScore = 7 - jScore
        testRecords.push({
          userId,
          testType: "mbti",
          resultType: mbtiType,
          resultTypeName: `${mbtiType}`,
          scores: { E: eScore, I: iScore, S: sScore, N: nScore, T: tScore, F: fScore, J: jScore, P: pScore },
          createdAt: randDate(createdAt, "2026-02-10"),
        })
      }

      // 九型人格测试记录
      if (Math.random() < 0.7) {
        const scores: Record<string, number> = {}
        for (let t = 1; t <= 9; t++) {
          scores[String(t)] = t === enneagramType ? randInt(14, 20) : randInt(4, 14)
        }
        testRecords.push({
          userId,
          testType: "enneagram",
          resultType: String(enneagramType),
          resultTypeName: `${enneagramType}号`,
          scores,
          createdAt: randDate(createdAt, "2026-02-10"),
        })
      }

      // 数字生命密码测试记录
      if (Math.random() < 0.6) {
        testRecords.push({
          userId,
          testType: "numerology",
          resultType: String(lifePathNumber),
          resultTypeName: `生命灵数${lifePathNumber}`,
          scores: { lifePathNumber },
          birthday,
          createdAt: randDate(createdAt, "2026-02-10"),
        })
      }
    }

    // 批量写入
    if (users.length > 0) {
      await usersCol.insertMany(users)
    }
    if (testRecords.length > 0) {
      await testCol.insertMany(testRecords)
    }

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        usersCreated: users.length,
        testRecordsCreated: testRecords.length,
      },
    })
  } catch (error: unknown) {
    console.error("[知己Admin] 种子数据生成失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "生成失败: " + (error as Error).message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

import { useState, useEffect } from "react"
import { Users, BookOpen, UserCheck, FileText, TrendingUp, Activity, Database, Loader2 } from "lucide-react"

interface DashboardStats {
  totalUsers: number; totalTests: number; totalConsultants: number; totalReports: number; todayUsers: number; todayTests: number
}

export default function AdminDashboard() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<DashboardStats>({ totalUsers: 0, totalTests: 0, totalConsultants: 0, totalReports: 0, todayUsers: 0, todayTests: 0 })
  const [recentUsers, setRecentUsers] = useState<Record<string, unknown>[]>([])
  const [recentTests, setRecentTests] = useState<Record<string, unknown>[]>([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [seeding, setSeeding] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => { fetchDashboard() }, [])

  const fetchDashboard = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/admin/dashboard")
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) {
        setStats(data.data.stats)
        setRecentUsers(data.data.recentUsers)
        setRecentTests(data.data.recentTests)
      }
    } catch (err) { console.error("获取仪表盘数据失败:", err) }
    finally { setLoading(false) }
  }

  /** 生成种子数据 */
  const handleSeedData = async () => {
    if (!confirm("确认生成2000条模拟用户数据？（含MBTI/九型人格/数字生命密码测试结果）")) return
    setSeeding(true)
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/admin/seed", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ count: 2000 }),
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) {
        alert(`生成成功！用户：${data.data.usersCreated}条，测试记录：${data.data.testRecordsCreated}条`)
        fetchDashboard()
      } else {
        alert("生成失败：" + data.error)
      }
    } catch { alert("网络错误") }
    finally { setSeeding(false) }
  }

  const statCards = [
    { label: "总用户数", value: stats.totalUsers, icon: Users, color: "from-coral to-orange", today: stats.todayUsers },
    { label: "总测试数", value: stats.totalTests, icon: BookOpen, color: "from-violet-500 to-purple-400", today: stats.todayTests },
    { label: "咨询师", value: stats.totalConsultants, icon: UserCheck, color: "from-emerald-500 to-teal-400", today: 0 },
    { label: "解读报告", value: stats.totalReports, icon: FileText, color: "from-amber-500 to-orange-400", today: 0 },
  ]

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground">数据概览</h1>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
          {[1, 2, 3, 4].map((i) => (
            <div key={i} className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur rounded-2xl p-6 animate-pulse border border-orange-100">
              <div className="h-4 bg-orange-100 rounded w-20 mb-4" />
              <div className="h-8 bg-orange-100 rounded w-16" />
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground">数据概览</h1>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <button onClick={handleSeedData} disabled={seeding}
            className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 bg-white/80 border border-orange-200 rounded-xl text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:border-coral/30 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50">
            {seeding ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Database className="w-4 h-4" />}
            {seeding ? "生成中..." : "生成2000条模拟数据"}
          </button>
          <button onClick={fetchDashboard} className="px-4 py-2 bg-white/80 border border-orange-200 rounded-xl text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors">
            刷新数据
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 统计卡片 */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
        {statCards.map((card) => {
          const Icon = card.icon
          return (
            <div key={card.label} className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur rounded-2xl border border-orange-100 p-6 hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-orange-100/30 transition-all">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
                <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{card.label}</span>
                <div className={`w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center shadow-md`}>
                  <Icon className="w-5 h-5 text-white" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="text-3xl font-bold text-foreground mb-1">{card.value.toLocaleString()}</div>
              {card.today > 0 && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-emerald-600">
                  <TrendingUp className="w-3 h-3" />
                  <span>今日 +{card.today}</span>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )
        })}
      </div>

      {/* 最近数据 */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur rounded-2xl border border-orange-100 p-6">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4">
            <Users className="w-5 h-5 text-coral" />
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground">最近注册用户</h2>
          </div>
          {recentUsers.length > 0 ? (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {recentUsers.slice(0, 5).map((user, index) => (
                <div key={index} className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-b border-orange-50 last:border-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-coral/20 to-orange/20 flex items-center justify-center text-xs text-coral font-medium">
                      {String(user.nickname || "用户").charAt(0)}
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-foreground">{String(user.nickname || "匿名用户")}</div>
                      <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{String(user.phone || "")} · {String(user.mbtiType || "-")}</div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{String(user.createdAt || "").slice(0, 10)}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="text-center py-8 text-muted-foreground text-sm">暂无用户数据<br /><span className="text-xs">点击上方"生成2000条模拟数据"按钮</span></div>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur rounded-2xl border border-orange-100 p-6">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4">
            <Activity className="w-5 h-5 text-violet-500" />
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground">最近测试记录</h2>
          </div>
          {recentTests.length > 0 ? (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {recentTests.slice(0, 5).map((test, index) => {
                const typeColors: Record<string, string> = { mbti: "text-violet-600 bg-violet-50", enneagram: "text-emerald-600 bg-emerald-50", numerology: "text-amber-600 bg-amber-50" }
                const typeLabels: Record<string, string> = { mbti: "MBTI", enneagram: "九型人格", numerology: "数字密码" }
                return (
                  <div key={index} className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-b border-orange-50 last:border-0">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                      <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-medium ${typeColors[String(test.testType)] || "text-gray-600 bg-gray-50"}`}>
                        {typeLabels[String(test.testType)] || test.testType}
                      </span>
                      <span className="text-sm text-foreground">{String(test.resultTypeName || test.resultType || "-")}</span>
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{String(test.createdAt || "").slice(0, 10)}</span>
                  </div>

            <div className="text-center py-8 text-muted-foreground text-sm">暂无测试记录</div>

    </div>
  )
}
